Table: GRB Peak Flux Spectra fit by SBPL Function
================================================================================
Byte-by-byte Description of file: datafile5B.txt
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
   Bytes Format Units           Label   Explanations
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
   1-  4 I4     ---            Tnum    Trigger number
   6-  9 A4     ---            Dets    Detectors used
  11- 14 A4     ---            Dtype   Datatype 
  16- 21 F6.2   s              Time    Total integrated time
  23- 30 E8.2   ph/s/cm2/keV   Amp     Amplitude
  32- 39 E8.2   ph/s/cm2/keV e_Amp     Uncertainty in Amp
  41- 47 F7.2   ---            Alpha   Low-Energy Spectral Index
  49- 55 F7.2   ---          e_Alpha   Uncertainty in Alpha 
  57- 63 F7.2   ---            Beta    High-Energy Spectral Index
  65- 71 F7.2   ---          e_Beta    Uncertainty in Beta
  73- 80 E8.2   keV            Ebreak  Spectral Break Energy
  82- 89 E8.2   keV          e_Ebreak  Uncertainty in Ebreak
  91- 98 E8.2   keV            Epeak   Peak of nuFnu Spectrum
 100-107 E8.2   keV          e_Epeak   Uncertainty in Epeak
 109-115 F7.2   ph/s/cm2       Pflux   Photon Flux
 117-123 F7.2   ph/s/cm2     e_Pflux   Uncertainty in Pflux
 125-131 F7.2   ph/cm2         Pflnc   Photon Fluence
 133-139 F7.2   ph/cm2       e_Pflnc   Uncertainty in Pflnc
 141-149 E9.2   mW/m2          Eflux   Energy Flux
 151-159 E9.2   mW/m2        e_Eflux   Uncertainty in Eflux
 161-169 E9.2   mJ/m2          Eflnc   Energy Fluence
 171-179 E9.2   mJ/m2        e_Eflnc   Uncertainty in Eflnc
